implemented across multiple Go source files in the kubernetes/kubernetes repository. The core admission framework is located in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/, while Kubernetes-specific plugins are registered in pkg/kubeapiserver/.\\n\\n## Core Admission Framework\\n\\n**Interface Definition and Registration** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/interfaces.go):\\n- Defines the `Interface` interface with `Handles()` method for checking operation support\\n- Defines `MutationInterface` with `Admit()` method for mutating plugins\\n- Defines `ValidationInterface` with `Validate()` method for validating plugins\\n- Defines `Attributes` interface containing request information and `ReinvocationContext` for tracking re-invocations\\n\\n**Plugin Management** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugins.go):\\n- `Plugins` registry manages admission plugin registration and instantiation\\n- `NewFromPlugins()` method creates the admission chain from a list of plugin names\\n- Separates mutating plugins from validating plugins for ordered execution\\n\\n## Admission Chain Execution\\n\\n**Chain Implementation** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/chain.go):\\n- `chainAdmissionHandler` is a slice of `Interface` implementations that executes plugins sequentially\\n- `Admit()` method calls `MutationInterface.Admit()` on each handler that handles the operation\\n- `Validate()` method calls `ValidationInterface.Validate()` on each handler in order\\n- Returns immediately on first error from any handler\\n\\n**Re-invocation Support** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/reinvocation.go):\\n- `reinvoker` wraps the admission chain to support re-invocation based on `ReinvocationContext`\\n- `newReinvocationHandler()` creates this wrapper\\n- Calls mutating plugins twice if `ShouldReinvoke()` returns true, supporting webhook reinvocation policies\\n\\n## Mutating Admission Webhooks\\n\\n**Webhook Plugin** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go):\\n- `Plugin` implements `admission.MutationInterface`\\n- `Register()` registers the \\\"MutatingAdmissionWebhook\\\" plugin\\n- `NewMutatingWebhook()` creates instances using `generic.NewWebhook()`\\n\\n**Configuration Management** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go):\\n- `mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager` implements `generic.Source` interface\\n- `NewMutatingWebhookConfigurationManager()` creates manager that watches MutatingWebhookConfiguration resources\\n- Maintains list of webhook accessors and notifies on changes\\n\\n**Dispatcher** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go):\\n- `mutatingDispatcher` implements `generic.Dispatcher` interface\\n- `Dispatch()` iterates through webhook list and calls individual webhooks\\n- Applies JSON patches from webhook responses to the request object\\n- Handles re-invocation markers for webhook re-invocation policy\\n\\n## Validating Admission Webhooks\\n\\n**Webhook Plugin** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go):\\n- `Plugin` implements `admission.ValidationInterface`\\n- `Register()` registers the \\\"ValidatingAdmissionWebhook\\\" plugin\\n- `NewValidatingAdmissionWebhook()` creates instances using `generic.NewWebhook()`\\n\\n**Configuration Management** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go):\\n- `validatingWebhookConfigurationManager` implements `generic.Source` interface\\n- `NewValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager()` creates manager that watches ValidatingWebhookConfiguration resources\\n- Maintains list of webhook accessors and notifies on configuration changes\\n\\n**Dispatcher** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go):\\n- `validatingDispatcher` implements `generic.Dispatcher` interface\\n- `Dispatch()` iterates through webhook list and calls individual webhooks\\n- Does not modify the object (read-only validation)\\n- Returns rejection errors from webhooks immediately\\n\\n## Generic Webhook Infrastructure\\n\\n**Webhook Base** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go):\\n- `Webhook` type provides common infrastructure for both mutating and validating webhooks\\n- `NewWebhook()` creates generic webhooks with configurable source (config manager) and dispatcher\\n- Handles webhook client management, authorization checking, and CEL condition evaluation\\n\\n## Kubernetes-Specific Configuration\\n\\n**Plugin Registration** (pkg/kubeapiserver/options/plugins.go):\\n- `RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()` registers all kube-apiserver admission plugins\\n- `AllOrderedPlugins` defines execution order: mutating plugins first, then validating plugins\\n- Mutating webhooks execute before validating webhooks\\n- Admission policies (CEL-based) execute in their own positions\\n\\n**Server Integration** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/admission.go):\\n- `AdmissionOptions.ApplyTo()` creates the admission chain and sets it on the server config\\n- Initializes all plugin initializers including generic and Kubernetes-specific ones\\n- Wraps the chain with metrics decorator via `admissionmetrics.WithStepMetrics()`\\n\\n## Request Handler Integration\\n\\nThe admission chain is called at request handling time:\\n\\n- **Create Handler** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/create.go):\\n  - Calls mutating admission via `mutatingAdmission.Admit(ctx, admissionAttributes, scope)`\\n  - Calls validating admission via handlers\\n\\n- **Update Handler** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/update.go):\\n  - Calls mutating and validating admission for UPDATE operations\\n\\n- **Patch Handler** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/patch.go):\\n  - Calls mutating and validating admission for PATCH operations\\n\\n- **Delete Handler** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/delete.go):\\n  - Calls admission for DELETE operations\\n\\n- **REST Handler** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/rest.go):\\n  - Calls admission for CONNECT operations\\n\\n- **Field Manager** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/fieldmanager/admission.go):\\n  - `NewManagedFieldsValidatingAdmissionController()` wraps admission to validate managed fields\\n\\nThe execution order ensures mutating plugins run first to modify the request, followed by validating
